< Text>
This is a genuine emergency facility to take your animal in the middle of the night for a real emergency. They are only open when most vets are closed, something like 8pm to 8am, but don't quote me on that. They are very kind but more importantly they understand triage and know what do in an emergency situation. You can call them if need be and tell them your situation and they might be able to give you advice if you unsure how to proceed. Its not cheap, but they'll tell you costs as quickly as they can. They don't over charge as far as I'm concerned. Expect to pay minimum $300 if they begin to work on your animal. They are very competent and they truly care, but just understand bills can get high very quickly so tell them if you have limited funds. We feel lucky to have to this place so close. We've had to use them a few times and I don't know what we would have done if they weren't around.<//Text>

< Review>
This clinic would rather let a pet suffer than accept a payment from another family member for emergency surgery. My brother needed to have emergency surgery on his cat that would cost between $1000 - $2000+. Insurance will cover it once he declares the expense, but we have to pay upfront. My brother unfortunately did not have this disposable income so he called me for help and was referred to eagle rock from the initial testing clinic who recommended immediate emergency surgery. I live in Chicago and cannot get to LA in time (At midnight), but gave my brother all the necessary credit card information he needed to pay for surgery thinking we live in a modern world with global financial practices....BUT They would not let him pay as he is not the cardholder and they refused him when he asked them to talk to me (the cardholder) on the phone and accept my information needed, including my ID card, and a signed letter of authorization, which they didnt have.
WHO DOESN'T HAVE AN AUTHORIZATION LETTER FOR THESE SITUATIONS!? ITS STANDARD PRACTICE!
They were not interested and turned him away, giving him the name of other clinics to call. This all at 10pm when my brother is freaking out and having to drive through L.A to find someone who accepts my card or has an authorization form and time is of the essence. My brother has payed over $1200 dollars already and is desperately trying to save his cat. After all. We own pets as companions, care about our animals, and they become family.

Shame on you Eagle Rock! This is when people need you most and especially when time is a big factor for survival. Feel free to message me if you have an answer as your reasoning you gave my brother was laughable and quite frankly a joke. I own 2 businesses and never in my life have not accepted payment because I was scared a client would ask for their money back... People in this world may sometimes be dishonest, but maybe work on your business controls and processes because not having a credit card authorization form for situations like this FYI, is archaic for 2018.
Thankfully, I enjoy staying up until 2am on a Wednesday/Thursday night when I have to get up tomorrow at 7am. Well thats what family is for, and our pets are family.

Another clinic not too far away had a credit card authorization form and we are crossing fingers and praying that toot the cat will be ok by tomorrow.

Disclaimer: Now just so you all know this is not just a rant that doesn't take all factors into consideration. This review DOES NOT describe their medical abilities and or discredit any of the positive reviews on this page. It also doesn't speak to the clinics know how, as I am sure their doctors are more than capable and educated in their field. This is however, the first impression they gave. THE WORST in my opinion, as it should be pet forward thinking. So if you want to save your pet or have an emergency. Go somewhere else, as they wont work with you to find a solution if it doesn't fit their limited business know how. If you have no constraints as a pet owner, and need or want to come here, then great! I hope they are better with their care than they are with their customer service when it comes to emergency situations. JUST READ THE 1 STAR REVIEWS. You will see a pattern!</Review>

< Text>
Roof Replacement
Avoid this business. They did a bait & switch on us, then tried to convince us that the lesser quality materials used were of equal or better quality. I explained to them that we agreed to premium quality materials at a premium price. They delivered and installed a lesser quality material. When I called them on it, several of their staff tried to convince me that the lesser quality material was just as good. Four people from their office came over to my house to explain to us that we got what we agreed too. They presented the original contract that we had signed to show that we agreed to a lesser quality material. I then presented my copy of the contract. My copy of the contract no longer matches the original contract. They had altered the original contract without our knowledge or permission to reflect a lesser quality material. I asked them to lower the overall cost to reflect the lesser quality material that they had already installed on my house. They refused to lower the price, so I had them remove the entire roof for a second time and start over again with material that I agreed upon first.
Additionally, no inspections were made and no permit was taken out until I called them on not pulling a permit. The job was completed and then a blank permit was delivered to my house. As of this writing, no city inspector has inspected the already completed job.
I have already filed formal complaints with both the Better Business Bureau and the Calif. State contractors licensing board.

<user_id>105773200051794568202< /user_id>< Review>
If I could give this place less than one star, I would. If Google reviews had black holes for bad reviews, I would push this place past the event horizon.

Do not shop at this rip-off establishment.

A few days ago my girlfriend and I bought two iPhones there at an OK price. The salesperson sold us cases and screen protectors for the phones. We did not ask the prices for those, but I am willing to pay more than the Amazon price to support a local business. They also sold us one pair of earbuds. We did not know that the regular iPhone earbuds were in the boxes with the phones. The salesperson said the earbuds were regularly $120, but we would get them for $70.

When we got home we found out that we had been charged $119.96 for the cases and covers, that we did not need extra earbuds, that the earbuds we had bought should retail for about $30, and that the most expensive iPhone 11 screen protectors on Amazon are $20 for a two-pack. The packaging for the screen protectors was not in the bag with the iPhone boxes, earbuds and receipts.

When we returned to the store today, the salesperson told us he had done everything correctly, that $29.99 each was the correct price for the screen protectors and cases, and that the earbuds were not returnable, even though the package had not been opened. When I asked to speak to the manager, the salesperson claimed to be the manager and owner of the store. Another Cricket store told us later that they sell an iPhone 11 screen protector for $14.99. I am going to guess that price is for a two-pack.

I got no help from Cricket phone and chat support. They told me to return to the store and ask for the manager. They could not give me the name of the store owner, nor could they verify that the salesperson's name on the purchase receipt matched the name of the owner.

One can accept the $30 price for each case and add another $30 for screen protectors (rather high prices, but legitimate). That comes to $90 that we should have been charged. The total charge for the earbuds we don't want, the cases, and the protectors was $190. This store ripped us off for $100.

Let me repeat. This store overcharged us by $100 and refused to make it right.

Rip-off establishment. Do not shop there!<//Review>

<Rate>5< /Rate>< Text>
For many, many years, fear was instilled when it came to fathoming dental procedures. I never wanted to go, and i hardly ever went!  That was probably a bad decision.
Fortunately, my 1st cavity came when I was 21... so, I got that fixed, but was then told ALL 4 of my wisdom teeth needed to be pulled out as well!! OMG? WHAAT??
My 1st super wise tooth was the WORST ever... !! The DDS told me NOT to look just prior to administering the anesthesia, and of course - what did i do?! - I looked!! That caused me to hyperventilate and freak out AND even cry!! (and i'm NO cry baby)... that set my underlying-instilled "fears" in stone haha

After that experience, the field of dentistry was on a demise for me!! I avoided the dentist for 10 years!!! Sadly, it was 10 years too long...

I must say, I did not anticipate the kindness and gentleness of this practice I only recently discovered. I had a free consult with x-rays on my 1st visit, then we discussed a treatment plan. There was NO pressure, and the staff is AMAZING!!! Those ladies make you feel exceptionally comfortable.

Finally, most importantly! The reason I freaked out when I was young was because the DDS was NOT very gentle!  & honestly, I just felt very uncomfortable!
Dr Schneider is quite gentle. I didn't even realize he was numbing me up when he did!  He gave me NO real warning and just kept me calm. That is VITAL!!
Being a medical professional, this type of bedside manner is the most reputable. I am happy to say I have a dentist! (whereas before i really felt like i didn't need one haha)... I NEED 1!

I am so content with this facility that you can bet your sweet bottom teeth that I'll be biting my way back in there very soon (mostly because they SAY i should hahaha)

For excellent quality care, go see Kurt & his amazing staff!
I  promise you wont be disappointed. <3 :)< /Text>

<Time>1613888562110< /Time><Rate>5</Rate><review>I was doing some home hunting in the area and looked for a good bite to eat and came across the gorgeous photos for Bites & Bashes. Oddly, what caught my eye out of all the items was the Korean Breakfast plate - a mixture of white rice, bulgogi, and eggs. It seemed so simple yet the pictures looked so gorgeous and I had to try and see if the taste matched the picture quality, and it did!

My Korean Breakfast plate variation was with egg whites (+$1 extra), white rice, and bulgogi. I loved the presentation full of small colorful flakes, making the egg whites (which I know are usually boring - I cook them every morning, so I would know!) into a really nice treat. What should otherwise be a simplistic plate turned out to be really nice and flavorful. The egg whites were fluffy. The white rice was cooked just right (not too soft or hard), and the bulgogi was super flavorful and juicy mixed with onions and giving flavor to the rest of the rice and egg whites. My only small observation was that it was a bit pricy compared to other locations with similar bowls although the flavor profile and attention to detail make sense. I'd love to see some hot sauce or gochujang included though to give it a bit more of a bold flavor profile.

Parking is a little tight. There is some parking in the back of the restaurant as well as street / neighborhood parking (note the neighborhood is a bit narrow street-wise).

The cashier was super nice, and it looked like they were doing a major photo shoot inside. There is also some outdoor seating.

Hope to come back in the near future to try some other dishes!< /review><pictures>None<//pictures>< Response>

<username>Stephanie Lu</username><time>1579603563022<//time><Rating>5< /Rating><Review>- B R E A K D O W N (# of + stars = rating)
* A T M O S P H E R E/C O N C E P T: +1 star
* F O O D/P R E S E N T A T I O N: +1 star
* P O R T I O N/C O S T: +1 star
* S E R V I C E: +1 star
* R E V I S I T: +1 star

This unbelievably hip and cute cafe is located in Lomita and I hope it‚Äôs here to stay! I loved all the food and drink explanations + the excitement behind all the dishes. The mother was the chef and she came out to make sure we were okay and enjoying the food. She was very proud to say that she raised her children on the food she had just made us. Delicious food from mama, I loved it. Everything had a comforting, yet complex flavor to each dish without anything overpowering each other.

In addition, I loved the vegan aspect of the drinks because they don‚Äôt use egg whites, they use aquafaba which is apparently a pea. It was fun learning about this new frothy trick from the owner! It‚Äôs definitely safe to bring your vegan pals here.

The crack fries were aptly named as they were definitely made with crack. ;)

They also add colorful flowers to drinks and dishes which I am always a huge fan of. I love color blasts in my food and there‚Äôs many to delight your eyes here! Thanks for the wonderful experience!

P A R K I N G:

It‚Äôs pretty crowded in the residential area so you may have to foot it. I suggest carpooling.< /Review><pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMKJBpC1ptlNpch_35Gwr46O5zKmx4AGnwHK2LA=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /pictures><resp>None<//resp>< gmapID>

Cute little place. Beautiful open cafe to work - lots of natural light.

The lavender coffee is on point - rich, strong, and overall wonderful. I also had a turkey sandwich which was delicious. They really packed on the meat (I appreciate it!). They added some korean style pickled vegetables on the side which was a nice and complimentary touch.

The chef stopped by to check in on me which was kind of her. Made you feel welcome. I didn't get a chance to try the baked goods but they looked good! Very bite sized.

My only =( is that a sandwich and a coffee cost me $21 including tip. It's a bit steep for a meal!<//review>

<pics>None<//pics>< Text>
It's a nice, open room with plenty of tables and may even work for larger groups.
I knew before we arrived I'd be trying the Mama's Bolognese spaghetti and the Crack fries, she got the Asian Chicken Salad as there are few healthy choices for someone watching carbs.
So the first thing I tasted was the Crack fries and they didn't disappoint. She tried one which was her first mistake. They held true to their name and she struggled to keep her hands off.
Then there was the Bolognese spaghetti, real comfort food made with love. I already knew this was going to be one of my favorite places when suddenly she threw us a curve. She came out of the kitchen with a sample plate she wanted me to try. It was a churro pancake with whip cream and Jack Daniels syrup. Oh My God!!!
Anyway she didn't do well on her low carb diet today and I found a new favorite place to have lunch. She said the salad was refreshing and light. She would do it again.
The staff is super friendly and you won't go a minute without seeing them by your table.
We spent $14.50 for the salad, $16.00 for the spaghetti, $5.00 for the fries and $3.00 each for the tropical ice tea (also really good).
So $45.44 before tip so a little high for lunch but well worth it. I'm just gonna start telling people to try this because I'm impressed.< /Text>
